interview call in 2023 for MBA Program? Interview call is depend on the composite

Diversity. However, the lowest CAT
percentile for an engineering student from
EWS Category is 66.00.

Score, Work Experience and Gender
Diversity. However, the lowest CAT

NC-OBC Category is 55.92.

Point No. Query Reply
1 I am writing to address the circumstances
surrounding my participation in the Senior Technical
Assistant (CSE) examination held on August 28, 2023.
My application number for this exam is
R0123STC10029.
During the examination, I encountered a predicament
pertaining to the trade test section, specifically in the
context of the Frontend development portion. As
outlined in the examination paper, candidates were
presented with the option to select from either pure
JavaScript, React, or Angular for constructing the
Frontend. Based on this information, I opted to
proceed with React Js for the task at hand. However,
upon attempting to initiate the creation of a React
Project, I discovered that the system was equipped
with Node version 12, whereas a minimum of Node
version 14 is requisite for developing a React
Application.
Recognizing the significance of this issue, I promptly
brought it to the attention of the invigilators
approximately 25 minutes prior to the conclusion of
the examination. Over the course of this duration, I
was visited by staff members on three separate
occasions, who confirmed the inadequacy of the
installed Node version and assured me that steps
were being taken to rectify the situation. Regrettably,
merely moments before the culmination of the 40-
minute skill test, a staff member advised me to solely
utilize JavaScript for the task. This directive was
provided without due clarification in relation to the
initial choice offered in the question paper, and I was No such information is available
The applicant has sought clarification. Whereas
“information” does not include “clarification(s)” as
defined under Section 2(f) of RTI Act, 2005.
Definition of information under Section 2(f) of RTI
Act, 2005:
“information” means any material in any form,
including records, documents, memos, emails,
opinions, advices, press releases, circulars, orders,
logbooks, contracts, reports, papers, samples,
models, data material held in any electronic form and
information relating to any private body which can
be accessed by a public authority under any other law
for the time being in force.
Indian Institute of Technology Jodhpur
NH-62, Nagaur Road, Karwad, Jodhpur-342030

left with a mere five minutes to adapt my approach
accordingly.
While I am content with my performance in the
written portion of the examination, it is disheartening
to note that due to the unavailability of the requisite
software version, I encountered substantial
impediments during the trade test. As a result, I
incurred a loss of 25 marks. This situation has placed
my candidacy in a precarious position.
In light of these circumstances, I kindly request
clarification on the following matters:
Despite the syllabus explicitly mentioning React and
Angular as viable topics for examination, and the
examination paper affirming the freedom to select a
preferred framework for Frontend development, it
remains unclear why the appropriate Node version
was not installed on the system provided.
Additionally, if the intention was to confine Frontend
development to pure JavaScript exclusively, it raises
concerns as to the purpose of offering a choice in the
question paper. Furthermore, the directive to limit
myself to JavaScript was issued a mere five minutes
before the conclusion of the examination, leaving me
with insufficient time to adapt my approach
effectively.
I trust that your attention to these matters will
contribute to a fair and comprehensive
understanding of the challenges I encountered during
the examination. Your clarification on the points
raised above would greatly assist in addressing the
discrepancies that have arisen.
f you are not satisfied with the information provided, you can
ppeal to the First Appellate Authority, by submitting online application through RTI portal and alternatively you

concerns as to the purpose of offering a choice in the
question paper. Furthermore, the directive to limit
myself to JavaScript was issued a mere five minutes
before the conclusion of the examination, leaving me
with insufficient time to adapt my approach
effectively.

contribute to a fair and comprehensive
understanding of the challenges I encountered during
the examination. Your clarification on the points
raised above would greatly assist in addressing the
discrepancies that have arisen.

08 December 2023
This is with reference to your RTI Application received in the Institute in hard copy. As per
the provisions of the RTI ACT a prescribed fee of Rs. 10 is to be deposited for seeking information. 
Exemption of fee is available to persons under BPL category. It is apprised that neither you have 
provided a Postal Order of Rs. 10 as RTI Fee along with the application nor submitted proof for 
exemption of fee.
In view of the above and as per the Guidelines for information seekers under the Right to
Information Act, 2005, “the applicant along with the application, should send a demand draft or a banker’s 
cheque or an Indian Postal Order of Rs. 10/- to the Public Authority as fee prescribed for seeking information 
and if the applicant belongs to below poverty line (BPL) category, he is not required to pay any fee. However, 
he should submit a proof in support of his claim to belong to the below poverty line”. Hence, for providing 
the information you are requested to provide documentary evidence for exemption from payment 
of fee or pay a prescribed fee of Rs. 10 through a Demand Draft or a Banker’s Cheque or an Indian 
Postal Order of Rs. 10/- payable in favour of “Director IIT Jodhpur”.

EWS/OBC/SC/ST, etc The Office of Students of IIT Jodhpur informs,
motivates, guides, and assists students in the
application process for various scholarships
or financial aid. Some of the available
scholarships include:

Scholarship Portal (NSP), based on eligibility.

(I). For SC: Top Class Education Scheme for
SC Students
(II). For ST: National Fellowship and
Scholarship for Higher Education of ST
Students – Scholarship
(III). For OBC/EBC/DNT: PM YASASVI
CENTRAL SECTOR SCHEME OF TOP
CLASS EDUCATION IN COLLEGE FOR
OBC, EBC AND DNT STUDENTS
For more details, please visit:
https://scholarships.gov.in/

students according to state guidelines. A few
of them are as below:
I. https://scholarship.up.gov.in/
II. https://scholarshipportal.mp.nic.in/
III. https://sso.rajasthan.gov.in/
IV. https://www.aicte-jk-scholarship-
gov.in/
V. https://pmsonline.bih.nic.in/
3.Fee Remission as per MoE guidelines.
SC/ST/PH students: Complete Tuition fee
waiver. Economically backward students
(income < ₹ 1 lakh): Full Tuition fee remission.
Economically backward students (income ₹ 1
lakh to ₹ 5 lakh): 2/3
Tuition fee remission.
4. Other scholarships (government and
private) are also provided based on students
eligibility.

10 Detailed details of government facilities to be
provided to students with disabilities Initiatives taken by IIT Jodhpur towards
empowerment of Persons with Disabilities (PWD)
for facilitating their participation in all walks of life
and enjoy their rights equally with dignity and
respect:
1. IIT Jodhpur is following reservation guidelines
for PWD candidates as per existing Government of
India norms as applicable from time to time.
2. An infrastructure support ramp along with a
railing is provided across the campus. The ramps
are also in the Sports Complex.
3. Lifts have been provided for all Academic
blocks, Hostel blocks and Campus quarters.
4. Medical clinic with well-equipped facilities 24*7
and night duty doctors/attendants. Ambulance
service is also provided 24*7 for all students.
5. IIT Jodhpur is encouraging the PWD students to
active participation in culture and sports activities
and initiated coaching camps in various sports and
games for them.
6. The Institute provides hostel accommodations to
students with disabilities on the ground floors for
easy access to services and resources in different
hostels located at the IIT campus.
7. Ramps, lifts and separate washrooms are
available in all the buildings of the Institute for the
convenience of students with disability.
8. The student Wellbeing Committee is especially
sensitive to the needs of students with disability
and provides the required psychological support.
9. Providing transport facilities for differently
abled students.
10. Scholarship for Students with Disabilities as per
GOI Guidelines.
11. The Institute is following the guidelines of ‘The
Rights of Persons with Disabilities (RPWD) Act,
2016 for the candidates belonging to PWD
category, like providing Scribe /compensatory
time for examination and easy access to classrooms
through ramps/lifts etc.
12. The Institute has the facility of ramps and lifts
for students and employees with disabilities in all
the academic buildings, residential buildings, and
student hostels.
Also, accessible toilets for disabled persons are
present in all the hostels and Academic Buildings.
In residential buildings these are constructed
based on the requirement.
11 Funds spent on e-learning The fund spent for e-learning can be viewed in the
‘S. No. 19 E-Journals of Intangible Assets’ (Sch-4)’
of Balance sheet of the Audited Annual Accounts
for the FY 2022-23. The annexure “B” is attached
herewith.

mentioned Table No. - 01.

Accounts for the F.Y. 2022-23. The annexure “A” is
attached herewith.
